    Refactor purge_url() (#1340)
    
    * Allow multiple URLs to be purged at once.
    * Use urllib.parse.urljoin() instead of format so the paths can
      omit the leading slash.
    * Use a request session to purge URLs. This should reduce the
      overhead of opening up a connection for each URL to purge.
    * Rename purge_url() to purge_urls().

commit 3bd1ad50e4ff7240300ab55500fcddb895428fd1
Author: Berker Peksag <berker.peksag@gmail.com>
Date:   2017-08-09 23:38:13 +0300

    Switch to use non-forked version of django-comments-xtd
    
    The version we've been using doesn't support new migrations
    so we can't write a data migration without proper
    migration files.
    
    The built-in comments application also doesn't have migrations
    so we had to switch to 'django_comments'.
    
    We have to use a forked version because of the following line
    in setup.py:
    
        install_requires=['Django>=1.6']
    
    This would install the latest stable version of Django which
    would break our application.

2	1	base-requirements.txt
1	1	pydotorg/settings/base.py

commit 17479c524b3c82a304d573915373c2bf98e8c7bb
Merge: ad9c222 ede581d
Author: Ned Deily <nad@python.org>
Date:   2017-07-28 14:57:35 -0400

    Merge pull request #1109 from ned-deily/update-keys
    
    bpo-30992: Remove Barry's obsolete MD5-signed key.

commit ede581dbb8107759c3775a7b481722d2c39598b2
Author: Ned Deily <nad@python.org>
Date:   2017-07-28 13:17:18 -0400

    bpo-30992: Remove Barry's obsolete MD5-signed key.
    
    Current versions of gpg refuse to import MD5 keys by default, rejecting
    the whole file.  The only such key:
    pub  1024R/ED9D77D5 1997-12-08 Barry A. Warsaw <bwarsaw@cnri.reston.va.us>
    was used to sign releases older than 2.6.  If needed, that key can still
    be found via the link to it (http://barry.warsaw.us/barrypub-gpg.asc)
    on the downloads page (https://www.python.org/downloads/).

212	801	static/files/pubkeys.txt

commit db08a5d589d759c5de25aa53dc4f557e87682d46
Author: Berker Peksag <berker.peksag@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-08-08 07:36:56 +0300

    Fix duplicate key error in /accounts/signup/
    
    IntegrityError was raised because django-allauth calls
    UserCreationForm.save() (after 19e9ec56a8289d964228931c0853086d99fef234)
    which means we were trying to register the same user twice.
    
    django-allauth fixed this by adding a separate method
    "signup" and deprecated the old behavior:
    
        https://github.com/pennersr/django-allauth/blob/master/allauth/account/forms.py#L197
    
    However, we actually do not need a custom form class. This
    also fixes the broken user forms in the admin interface.
    
    I've removed UserCreationForm and added new test cases
    introduced in 19e9ec56a8289d964228931c0853086d99fef234.
    
    According to Sentry, over 3000 errors were logged in the past
    two months:
    
        https://app.getsentry.com/python-software-foundation/production/group/67968313/
    
    Fixes #777

0	1	pydotorg/settings/base.py
12	8	users/admin.py
0	34	users/forms.py
0	54	users/tests/test_forms.py
44	1	users/tests/test_views.py
1	1	users/views.py

    in a separate terminal.
